<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Uribe" title="Álvaro Uribe">Álvaro Uribe</a>, <a href="/wiki/President_of_Colombia" title="President of Colombia">President of Colombia</a> (2002–2010)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Manuel_Santos" title="Juan Manuel Santos">Juan Manuel Santos</a>, <a href="/wiki/President_of_Colombia" title="President of Colombia">President of Colombia</a> (2010–present)</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="960" data-file-width="1440" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a></b>

<li>President – <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Correa" title="Rafael Correa">Rafael Correa</a>, <a href="/wiki/President_of_Ecuador" title="President of Ecuador">President of Ecuador</a> (2007–present)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1200" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> (<a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">Overseas Territory</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>)
<ul>
<li>Governor –
<ol>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alan_Huckle" title="Alan Huckle">Alan Huckle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Governor of the Falkland Islands">Governor of the Falkland Islands</a> (2006–2010)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ric_Nye&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ric Nye (page does not exist)">Ric Nye</a>, <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Governor of the Falkland Islands">Acting Governor of the Falkland Islands</a> (2010)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigel_Haywood" title="Nigel Haywood">Nigel Haywood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Governor of the Falkland Islands">Governor of the Falkland Islands</a> (2010–2014)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Head of Government – <a href="/wiki/Tim_Thorogood" title="Tim Thorogood">Tim Thorogood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Chief Executive of the Falkland Islands">Chief Executive of the Falkland Islands</a> (2008–2012)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="500" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Flag_of_Guyana.svg/23px-Flag_of_Guyana.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Flag_of_Guyana.svg/35px-Flag_of_Guyana.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Flag_of_Guyana.svg/46px-Flag_of_Guyana.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a></b>

<li>Prime Minister – <a href="/wiki/Sam_Hinds" title="Sam Hinds">Sam Hinds</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Guyana" title="Prime Minister of Guyana">Prime Minister of Guyana</a> (1999–2015)</li>

</li>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="540" data-file-width="1000" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Paraguay_%281990-2013%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a></b>
<ul>

</li>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/23px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/35px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/45px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a></b>

<li>Prime Minister –
<ol>

<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Chang" title="José Antonio Chang">José Antonio Chang</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Peru" title="Prime Minister of Peru">President of the Council of Ministers of Peru</a> (2010–2011)</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_state_leaders_in_2010&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 35em; -webkit-column-width: 35em; column-width: 35em; list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Eritrea only became independent in 1993.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Bahrain only became independent in 1971.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Brunei only became independent in 1984.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Hun Sen was titled Second Prime Minister in 1993–98.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The three-member Presidency Council was <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a> collectively, but this changed to the usual form of having just the president as head after the <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_governorate_elections,_2009" title="Iraqi governorate elections, 2009">2009 elections</a>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Kazakhstan only became independent in 1991.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The position of Chairman of the National Defence Commission was declared to be the <i>highest office of state</i> by the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_North_Korea" title="Constitution of North Korea">constitution</a> that came into effect in 1998.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Uzbekistan only became independent in 1991.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Saleh was <a href="/wiki/President_of_Yemen_Arab_Republic" title="President of Yemen Arab Republic">president</a> of <a href="/wiki/Yemen_Arab_Republic" title="Yemen Arab Republic">North Yemen</a> until 1990.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-10">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Transnistria only <a href="/wiki/Transnistrian_independence_referendum,_1991" title="Transnistrian independence referendum, 1991">declared</a> independence in 1991.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Montenegro only became independent in 2006.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-12">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Serbia only became independent in 2006.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Kosovo only <a href="/wiki/2008_Kosovo_declaration_of_independence" title="2008 Kosovo declaration of independence">declared</a> independence in 2008.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The seven-member Swiss Federal Council is head of state and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">government</a> collectively. As a party to the Council, the president serves solely in a <a href="/wiki/Primus_inter_pares#Switzerland" title="Primus inter pares"><i>primus inter pares</i></a> capacity for one year.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
